[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report describes a libFuzzer timeout occurring during PDF text [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction. The root cause is an **infinite loop in the PDPageTree.PageIterator [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor** when processing a malicious PDF with circular references in the page [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtree structure.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key findings from code analysis:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Location of the infinite loop**: The PageIterator constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m184[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m197[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses a while loop that recursively processes page tree nodes without tracking [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvisited nodes.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Missing circular reference detection**: Unlike PDFieldTree.FieldIterator which[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhas circular reference detection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPDFBOX-[0m[1;36m5044[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the PageIterator lacks this [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotection.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Existing protections don't help**:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mCOSObject.getObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m has protection against recursive dereferencing, but the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue is at the page tree structure level[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The class-level pageSet field is only used in the [0m[1;35mget[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method, not in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPageIterator[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Each iterator needs its own local tracking to avoid interference[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Proven solution pattern**: PDFieldTree.FieldIterator [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m129[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m implements[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe correct pattern using a Set backed by IdentityHashMap to detect and prevent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcircular references.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy Details[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix requires modifying the `PDPageTree.PageIterator` inner class to add [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcircular reference detection, following the exact pattern established in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDFieldTree.FieldIterator` for PDFBOX-[0m[1;36m5044[0m[39m.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Add Required Import[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `pdfbox/src/main/java/org/apache/pdfbox/pdmodel/PDPageTree.java`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd the following import after line [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere Collections is imported[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimport java.util.IdentityHashMap;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add Visited Nodes Tracking Field[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: Inside the PageIterator class, after line [0m[1;36m182[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter the queue field[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd a new instance variable:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m To prevent infinite loops caused by circular references in malformed PDFs[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Must use IdentityHashMap for reference-based equality checking[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate final Set<COSDictionary> visitedNodes = [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mCollections.newSetFromMap[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew IdentityHashMap<>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses IdentityHashMap for reference equality [0m[1;39m([0m[39m==[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of content equality [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- More efficient than HashMap for reference-based comparison[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tracks specific COSDictionary instances to prevent processing the same node [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple times[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Local to each iterator instance, ensuring thread safety and independence[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Modify the enqueueKids Method[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: Lines [0m[1;36m206[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m225[0m[39m in PDPageTree.java[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the entire enqueueKids method with:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate List<COSDictionary> [0m[1;35menqueueKids[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSDictionary node[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Check for circular reference before processing[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mvisitedNodes.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mLOG.error[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Page tree node already visited, skipping to avoid infinite [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mrecursion"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return Collections.EMPTY_LIST;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Mark node as visited[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mvisitedNodes.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Process the node[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misPageTreeNode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return [0m[1;35mgetKids[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    else[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode != null && [0m[1;35mCOSName.PAGE.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnode.getCOSName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.TYPE[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mqueue.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        else[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mLOG.error[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Page skipped due to an invalid or missing type [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode == null ? [0m[32m"[0m[32m([0m[32mnull[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m : [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnode.getCOSName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.TYPE[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return Collections.EMPTY_LIST;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key changes**:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Check before processing**: First check if the node is already in visitedNodes[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Early return**: If already visited, log an error and return empty list to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbreak the cycle[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Mark as visited**: Add the node to visitedNodes immediately after checking[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserve existing logic**: All existing functionality for valid PDFs remains [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Proven pattern**: This exact solution was successfully implemented for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDFieldTree in PDFBOX-[0m[1;36m5044[0m[39m to fix a similar stack overflow issue caused by circular[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal code changes**: Only adds [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m lines of new code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimport, field [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration, and circular reference check[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while preserving all existing [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No breaking changes**: Valid PDFs without circular references will behave [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentically. Only malformed PDFs with circular references are affected.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Performance**: IdentityHashMap provides [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lookup with reference-based [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequality, adding negligible overhead for the common case while preventing [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcatastrophic behavior for malicious input.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Thread-safe**: Each iterator instance has its own local visitedNodes set, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoiding threading issues that would occur with shared state.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Queue behavior unchanged**: Pages are still added to the queue in the same [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morder for valid PDFs[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Page tree traversal**: The breadth-first traversal logic in the constructor [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m184[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m197[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains identical[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Error handling**: Existing error logging for invalid page types is preserved[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **isPageTreeNode check**: The distinction between page tree nodes and page nodes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis maintained[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **getKids behavior**: The method for retrieving child nodes is unchanged[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Breaks circular references**: When a node is encountered a second time, it's [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskipped instead of processed again[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Prevents infinite loops**: The while loop in the constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m187[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m196[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill eventually terminate because visitedNodes grows monotonically[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Logs for debugging**: Error messages help identify malformed PDFs in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproduction[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Graceful degradation**: Instead of hanging indefinitely, the fuzzer will [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplete with some pages possibly skipped[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Duplicate pages skipped**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: In a malformed PDF with circular references, some pages might appear [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly once instead of multiple times[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: This is the desired behavior - it's better to skip duplicate [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing than to hang indefinitely[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Detection**: Error log messages will alert users to the issue[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Memory overhead**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Each iterator allocates a Set to track visited nodes[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The memory overhead is proportional to the number of unique page [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtree nodes, which is bounded by the PDF structure. For typical PDFs, this is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdozens to hundreds of nodes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cleanup**: The Set is garbage collected when the iterator is no longer [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferenced[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Different behavior for malformed PDFs**[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Malformed PDFs with circular references will be processed differently[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The previous behavior was to hang indefinitely [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtimeout[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so any [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferent behavior is an improvement[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Consistency**: This matches the behavior of PDFieldTree which also skips [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcircular references[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe PDFieldTree.FieldIterator implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m129[0m[39m in PDFieldTree.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovides the exact template:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate final Set<COSDictionary> set = [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mCollections.newSetFromMap[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew IdentityHashMap<>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate void [0m[1;35menqueueKids[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPDField node[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mqueue.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mset.add[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnode.getCOSObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode instanceof PDNonTerminalField[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        List<PDField> kids = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mPDNonTerminalField[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m node[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getChildren[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPDField kid : kids[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mset.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mkid.getCOSObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mLOG.error[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Child of field '[0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m' already exists elsewhere, ignored to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mavoid recursion"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                        [0m[1;35mnode.getFullyQualifiedName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            else[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35menqueueKids[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkid[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
